<s> the pigeon a fantasy in three acts persons of the play christopher wellwyn an artist ann his daughter guinevere megan a flower seller rory megan her husband ferrand an alien timson once a cabman edward bertley a canon alfred calway a professor sir thomas hoxton a justice of the peace also a police constable three humble men and some curious persons the action passes in wellwyn's studio and the street outside <\s>
<s> the first of april <\s>
<s> act i it is the night of christmas eve the scene is a studio flush with the street having a skylight darkened by a fall of snow <\s>
<s> there is no one in the room the walls of which are whitewashed above a floor of bare dark boards <\s>
<s> a fire is cheerfully burning <\s>
<s> on a model's platform stands an easel and canvas <\s>

<s> chairs and a long old fashioned settle under the window <\s>

<s> on a low table a russian samovar is hissing and beside it on a tray stands a teapot with glasses lemon sugar and a decanter of rum <\s>
<s> through a huge uncurtained window close to the street door the snowy lamplit street can be seen and beyond it the river and a night of stars <\s>
<s> the sound of a latchkey turned in the lock of the street door and ann wellwyn enters a girl of seventeen with hair tied in a ribbon and covered by a scarf <\s>

<s> shredding of her gloves she warms her hands <\s>

<s> the pigeon a fantasy in three acts persons of the play christopher wellwyn an artist ann his daughter guinevere megan a flower seller rory megan her husband ferrand an alien timson once a cabman edward bertley a canon alfred calway a professor sir thomas hoxton a justice of the peace also a police constable three humble men and some curious persons the action passes in wellwyn's studio and the street outside <\s>
<s> the first of april <\s>
<s> act i it is the night of christmas eve the scene is a studio flush with the street having a skylight darkened by a fall of snow <\s>
<s> there is no one in the room the walls of which are whitewashed above a floor of bare dark boards <\s>
<s> a fire is cheerfully burning <\s>
<s> on a model's platform stands an easel and canvas <\s>

<s> chairs and a long old fashioned settle under the window <\s>

<s> on a low table a russian samovar is hissing and beside it on a tray stands a teapot with glasses lemon sugar and a decanter of rum <\s>
<s> through a huge uncurtained window close to the street door the snowy lamplit street can be seen and beyond it the river and a night of stars <\s>
<s> the sound of a latchkey turned in the lock of the street door and ann wellwyn enters a girl of seventeen with hair tied in a ribbon and covered by a scarf <\s>
<s> leaving the door open she turns up the electric light and goes to the fire <\s>
<s> she throws of her scarf and long red cloak <\s>
<s> she is dressed in a high evening frock of some soft white material <\s>
<s> her movements are quick and substantial <\s>
<s> her face full of no nonsense is decided and sincere with deep set eyes and a capable well shaped forehead <\s>
<s> shredding of her gloves she warms her hands <\s>
